vardhamāna purāṇaṁ]


[p. 3]
[prathamāśvāsaṁ]

śrīmadbhavyāḷi cakraprakara sukhakaraṁ sarvamithyāndhakāra // VaPu.1.1a
stōmapradhvaṁsi bōdhāmaḷakiraṇa gaṇōdbhāsi mōkṣābjinī su // VaPu.1.1b
prēmaṁ syādvāda pūrvācaḷa samuditanāścaryavr̥ttābhirāmaṁ // VaPu.1.1c
hēmāṅgaṁ vardhamānāhimakaranatinirdōṣamaṁ māḻke nammoḷ // VaPu.1.1d [sragdhare]

aphavighaṭana kāraṇama // VaPu.1.2a
mmaghaṭita padabandha bandhurāḷaṅkr̥tiyaṁ // VaPu.1.2b
laghavāge pogaḻe pēḻdaṁ // VaPu.1.2c
raghuvaṁśa mahāpurāṇamaṁ śrīvijayaṁ // VaPu.1.2d [kandaṁ]


[p. 4]
sarasaprasanna mādhu // VaPu.1.3a

dhareyoḷage negaḻe śāntī // VaPu.1.5a

ādijinanāthacaritama // VaPu.1.6a

vidagdha matiyenipa nāgadēvakavīndraṁ // VaPu.1.8d [kandaṁ]


[p. 5]

[p. 8]

[va.] adentendoḍakhiḷa jaḷakarimakara timi timiṅgiḷagrāha nivaha saṁrambha-
kṣōbhaṇādīrṇaraṅgattaraṅga bhaṅgurataraṅgamāḷākīrṇa lavaṇavāridhi parikṣipta-
mumasaṅkhyāta dvīpasāgarasaṅkhyānakkādibhūtamumēkalakṣapramita pramāṇa-
yōjana viṣkambhamuṁ pūrvāparāyatapratita himavanmahā himavanniṣada-
nīḷarugmīśikhari nāmōddāma varṣadhara parvatāvabhāsiyuṁ tadanantarānta-
rāda sthita (?) bharata haimavata hari vidēha ramyaka hairaṇyavatairāvatābhidhāna-
kṣētra saptakābhirāmamuṁ gaṅgāsindhuprabhr̥ti mahānadī pravāhōpaśōbhi-
tamuṁ jambūvr̥kṣalāñchanamumāgi negartevettī jambūdvīpada naṭṭanaḍuve

[p. 31]
[tr̥tīyāśvāsaṁ]

ittaludātta bhāratamahītaḷadoḷ paripālipa nr̥saṁ // VaPu.3.1a
pattige janmabhūmi sakaḷartuphaḷakke vipākalōkama // VaPu.3.1b
tyuttama puṇyabhājanajanakke sabhājanamemba meyme me // VaPu.3.1c
yvettire rañjikuṁ janapadaṁ dorevetta suramyanāmadiṁ // VaPu.3.1d [utpalamālike]

dharaṇīmukhābjamenisuva // VaPu.3.2a
suramyake mogakke mūgu tānembantā // VaPu.3.2b
gire sogayisuvudu paudana // VaPu.3.2c
puraṁ samuttuṅga ramyaharmyaprakaraṁ // VaPu.3.2d [kandaṁ]

adanadaṭaṁ prajāpatimahīpatiyāḷvanaśēṣa maṅgaḷā // VaPu.3.3a
bhyudayaparamparā parigatōdayanā nr̥pakuñjarakke bē // VaPu.3.3b
ṭada satiyar jayāvatiyumā mr̥gabhūvatiyembaḷuṁ samu // VaPu.3.3c
nmada vanadantigiṁtiveraḍuṁ madalēkhegaḷemba māḻkeyiṁ // VaPu.3.3d [campakamāle]

[va.] antavaroḷā  mahānubhāvanēkībhāvadiṁ saṁsārasukhamaṁ 
kaḍeyāgadanteyanubhavisi

ā jayāvatige puṭṭidaṁ mahā // VaPu.3.4a
rājavaibhavapadōcitaṁ sutaṁ // VaPu.3.4b
tējamunnatikeyuṁ parākramaṁ // VaPu.3.4c
sājamāge vijayākhyanāmadiṁ // VaPu.3.4d [rathōddhataṁ]


[p. 32]
lōkaṁ guḍigaṭṭe mr̥gā // VaPu.3.5a

vyākr̥tayaśanatibaḷaṁ tripiṣṭakumāraṁ // VaPu.3.5d [kandaṁ]

[va.] antu viśākhabhūticaranappa sā sāmānikaṁ bandu vijayanemba

dēvanāgiyumavarge puṭṭa janmāntarānugata sahajasnēhadindondidorva-
rorvaroḷeccaḍaḻkaṟuṁ kūrmeyumadhikamāgi baḷeye

gurubhujagarvamarvisuva tējadagurvu  nayāgamakramaṁ // VaPu.3.6a

sarigoḷe pāṭi pāsaṭi samaṁ sarisaṅgoḷe pōlveyembinaṁ // VaPu.3.6d [campakamāle]

[va.] antā kumāradvayamaśēṣa lōkābhyarthitārthapratāna nidhāna-

daḷita dhavaḷābja muktā // VaPu.3.8a

[p. 33]

[va.] antanupamāna rūpaguṇasampattigaṁ yauvanōdāttavr̥ttigaṁ

[p. 35]

[va.] mattorme narmasaciva pradhāna prakr̥tipuruṣapravēka parivr̥taṁ

vittaṁ naimittakaṁ bandu nimma kiṟiyamaganī puruṣōttamaṁ tripiṣṭaṁ 
trikhaṇḍamaṇḍaḷādhipanamōghanakkumadakkaṁ kōṭikaśiḷāsamuddharaṇaṁ pratyaya-
mendaṟiye pēḻdu sabhāsadara sannidhānadoḷādēśapatramaṁ kuḍuvudamarasanati-
sambhramākrāntasvāntanāgi rāgisi daivajñanannādaramberasu mannisi kaḷipi 
katipayadinaṅgaḷiṁ nāmamudbhūtamaṁ nōḻpa kautūhaḷadiṁ vijayanuṁ

[va.] ondu divasamā kanne tannoḍanāḍigaḷumappa keḷadiyar suttiṟi-
doḍane bare sarōvarakke bappa marāḷamaṇḍaḷiyante nijajanakanāsthākkevandu 
tadīya padapayōjaṅgaḷanā nīḷakuṭiḷakuntaḷakaḷāpāvaḷiyādēyadinaḷaṁ 
karisi pādapīṭhōpakaṇṭhadoḷirda kanakamayaviṣṭaradoḷ kuḷḷirpuduṁ viyaccara-
rājanātmatanūjeyanaḻkaṟuverasu nōḍi

madiraṁ kēkara dr̥ṣṭivalgana saraṁ bhūribhramaṁ prauḍhigā // VaPu.3.46a

[p. 40]
[va.] antu kiṟidu pottu manadoḷe mantaṇamirdu niścayisalaṟi-
yade nāsahāyasya mantrasiddhiyembudaṁ bagedu nijavadanatāmbūḷapradāna-
pūrvakadiṁ bhūpati sabheyaṁ visarjisi parimitāptajana parijana parivr̥tanāgi 
vidvajjanadoḷirdu pēḻimī kanyāratnamenisida svayamprabheyanārge kuḍuva-
membudumavar tammoḷāḷōcisi bharaṅgeydu vidyādhara cakravarti mayūra-
grīvanagratanayanaśvagrīvanāgrahadiṁ palavu sūḻ bēḍiyaṭṭidamātanoḍamba-
ḍadannamārgaṁ kuḍalke bāradadu kāraṇadinī kāryamaṁ daivajñarapparaṁ 
besagoṇḍu negaḻvudene sambhinnanappa naimittikanaṁ barisi yathōcitācaraṇa-

[va.] antu bhavanimittagī negeda vibhaṅgajñānadiṁ narakagatiprāptiyana-

[va.] adalladeyuṁ mattavantavandiranorvaranagurvāge kabbina kōlgaḷaṁ 
kaḍivante sandhisandhidappade kaḍidaḍasi gāṇadoḷotti piḍideseyuṁ khaṇḍakhaṇḍa-
māge kiṟikiṟide kuṟidaṟiduṟidu tīvi kumbhīpākadoḷege pūḻdeḍeyu-
mativikaṭamāda śālmalīniśāta kaṇṭakāgradoḷiṭṭu karagasadiṁ sīḷvante saṟra 
saṟrane piḍidurceyuṁ taḷtaḷisi kudiva lōhadeṇṇeyoḷ kaḍimuṟukanāgirdu 
paṟiyalāgadantirisi suruḷe tāḷisiyuṁ miḍiyintoṭṭu peḍatalevaraṁ tidi-
yugidetti kōlaṁ patti sutti keṅgalisuva keṇḍadoḷ pūḻdu puṭapākaṁ 
suḍeyumatyāgrahamāgirpa tāḻaśūḷāgramanēṟalvēḻdu meygaḷirvasiyāgi 
soḍane nōḍe sōdanepōge baradegeyeyuṁ rōmarōmandappaderde-

nuṇṇidavappa saṇṇigegaḷoḷ saṇṇiseyumintasahyamappa nārakaduḥkhadiṁ jīvaṁ 
mr̥tāvastheyaneydi

[va.] antasaṁ tāge pantise basamaḻidu paṇta kekkariyante bikkane biri-

[va.] mattondu divasamā kaṇṭhīravanaviraḷa bahaḷa vaṁśa śiṁśapā śamī-
śirīṣa kiṁśukāśōka rasamyākaśālmōpaḷōpaprabhr̥ti bhūjarāji parikṣēpa-
doḷuccaḷadatucca nirjarōdāra śiśira jaḷaśīkarāsāra saṁsiktadoḷupanipatadabhi-
nava surabhikusuma pādapaprasūna mañjarīrajaḥprasara dūsarōpakaṇṭhadoḷu-

[va.] mattamā samyagdaruśanamanantānubandhi krōdha māna māyā-

parāyaṇarāgiyuṁ samarābhirivēśamaṁ bisuṭṭu śaraṇārthigaḷāgiyuṁ bandu 
cakrēśvaraṅgeṟagi kaṇḍu pādapīṭhōpakaṇṭhapradēśadoḷ meyyanikki

emmapavādamanommige // VaPu.9.59a

rthaṁ mattadu dēva ninagupāyanamātraṁ // VaPu.9.59d [kandaṁ]

[va.] antā mahābhāgadhēyanamēyaguṇamaṇiprarōhaṇanāgi diva-

ratnamuṁ saunandakamemba kaukṣēyakamuṁ caṇḍavēgamemba daṇḍaratnamuṁ

[p. 170]

yappa padmanidhiyuṁ maṇimayavicitra bhūṣaṇāvitaraṇaṅgeyva piṅgaḷamemba

māṇavakamumātōdyahr̥dyavādyaṅgaḷaṁ janiyisuva śaṅkhanidhiyuṁ kanaka-

kulavadhūjanamuṁ mūvatticchāsirvar pratyanta mlēccharājatanūjeyaruṁ 
mūvatticchāsirvaravaruddha vāranārīnikāyamumantu tombattārusāsirva-
rantaḥpurastrīyaruṁ mūvatticchāsirvar maigāpina gaṇabaddhadēvaruṁ mūvatti-

membattanālkukōṭi padātiyuṁ mūvatticchāsira viṣayaṅgaḷumanite prasiddha-
mahānagaraṅgaḷuṁ tombattāṟukōṭi grāmaṅgaḷumombaisāsiraṁ drōṇā-
mukhaṅgaḷuṁ nālvatteṇsāsira paṭṭaṇaṅgaḷuṁ padināṟusāsira khēḍaṅgaḷuṁ

gaḷumaṟunūṟu kukṣikanivāsaṅgaḷuṁ daśasahasrakōṭi halaṅgaḷuṁ mūṟu

[va.] antu jinarūpamanā priyamitrabhūpaṁ kaikoṇḍanantaraṁ kṣētra-

[p. 172]
vratadhāraṇaṁ samitipāḷanamemba lakṣaṇadiṁ neṟedu ninda saṁyamamuṁ
tannoḷaḷavaḍe tāḷdi mithyānidhāna māyāśalyaṅgaḷaṁ toṟedu vikathākaṣā-
yamindriyaprēma nidrāvikalpamappa padinaiduṁ pramādamaṁ pariharisi vina-
yēryāpathōtsarga śayana bhaikṣāsana vāṅmanaḥśarīraviṣayamappeṇṭuṁ śuddhi-
gaḷanappukeydu nityādi dvādaśānuprēkṣāsmaraṇadoḷ manamaniṭṭu kṣutpi-
pāsā śītōṣṇa daṁśa maśaka prabhr̥ti dvāviṁśatiparīṣahaṅgaḷaṁ sairisi daśakuśala-
dharmadoḷ niyatātmanāgi sāmāyikacchēdōpasthāpanā parihāraśuddhi-
cāritradoḷ kūḍe negaḻuttaṁ pratyākhyāna pratikramaṇādi ṣaḍvidhāvaśyakaṁ 
gaḷaṁ tappade palavukālaṁ tapōnuṣṭhānadoḷ niścayaṁ naḍedu jīvitāvasāna-
doḷ samādhividhiyiṁ kaḻidu niratiśayasukhaikasāradoḷ sahasrārakalpa-
doḷ sūryadhvajōpalakṣita rucakābhidhāna vimānadoḷ sūryaprabha-
nemboṁ dēvanāgi

[va.] intu banda madhusamayadoḷorvaṁ pūrvaparicitaṁ vanapāḷakaṁ 
bandu nūtana sujāta cūtaprasūnagucchamumanativiśāḷa pratinavalasa-
daśōka pravāḷajāḷamumanīṣadunmiṣanmallikāvallarī samudbhūta surabhitara-
mukuḷamumaṁ nikāma kōmaḷa rucira campakasugandhīkaḷikā nikāyamu-
manabhinavōjjr̥mbhamāṇōddāma viḷāviḷāsinī pūgamañjariyumaṁ tandu 
mundiṭṭanakṣaraṁ vasantada baravanaṟipi tadanantaraṁ vasantadoḍaneye mahā-
tapōdhanaravadhijñānigaḷ bandudyānavanavibhāgamanaḷaṅkarisirdarendudātta-
śrōtrāmr̥tākṣaranyāsadiṁ prōṣṭhilācāryara baravanaṟiye binnavise nandanaṁ 
nijānandadinānandananigaṅgacittamanitturadanākṣaṇadoḷe mahāmahimarve-

goṇḍu pūjisi gurubhaktikriyāpurassaraṁ bandisi tadīya caraṇāravinda-

[va.] antavaṟoḷagamāyurnāmakarmōdayanimittamātmanoḷādu-

tumaṁ samayōttarakramadiṁ kūḍe neraputtamutkr̥ṣṭasthitiyaneyde kaṭṭuvudu

dvitīyādi samayaṅgaḷoḷavaṁ biṭṭu bēṟevēṟe sūkṣmasnigdhādi bhēdabhinnaṁ

[va.] antacintya mahimātiśayadoḷ kūḍi dīkṣāgrahaṇadoḷ

kṣaṇāpahitanētranumaviḷambita drutapadakṣēpanumapāsta viḷāvikāra digavaḷō-

manegāgi bappāgaḷ

[va.] antu pañcāścaryaṅgaḷeseye navavidhapuṇyanuṁ śraddhādi saptaguṇa-

[va.] āgaḷumadhyātmadhyānādhīnanadhruvamaśaraṇaṁ saṁsāramēkatvama-
nyatvamaśuci lōkasthānamāsrava saṁvare nirjare bōdhidurlabhaṁ dharmasvākhyā-
tattvamendintivaṟoḷanuprēkṣegeyyuttamapramattaguṇasthānadoḷ nindu 
munnamājñāvicayamapāyavicaya vipākavicaya saṁsthānavicayamemba 
nālkuṁ dharmadhyānamaṁ dhyānisuttamatiśaya viśuddhalēśyātmakanāda pramattā
[p. 231]
pūrva nivr̥ttikaraṇa pariṇāmatritayadindanantānubandhi krōdha māna māyā-
lōbhaṅgaḷumaṁ mithyātva saṁyama samyagmithyātva samyaktvaprakr̥tiyemba 
darśanamōhatritayamumaṁ kramakramadiṁ kaḻalci kaḷedu saptaprakr̥tikṣayadiṁ 
kṣāyikadr̥ṣṭiyaṁ paḍedu tadanantaramantarmuhūrtadoḷaṁ pramattāpramatta-
parāvartanasahasradiṁ kṣapakaśrēṇi samārōhaṇābhimukha yathāprayōgaṁ 
tadyōgya trividhakaraṇapariṇataṁ pratisamayamasaṅkhyāta guṇahāni nirūpamappa 
nirjarāvidhiyindāyuṣyakarmavalladaśēṣa karmaprakr̥tisthityanubhavaṅgaḷaṁ kundi 
suttamanantaguṇaśaktikhacitaikapariṇāmanapūrvakaraṇaguṇasthāna niṣkāṇḍa-
nivr̥tti bādarasāmparāyakṣapaka guṇasthānasthitanantarmuhūrtaṅgaḷiṁ nidrā-
nidrā pracaḷāpracaḷā styānagr̥ddhi narakagati tatprāyōgyānupūrvatiryaggati -
tatprāyōgyānupūrvaka dvi tri caturindriya jātyātapōdyōta sthāvara-
sūkṣma sādhāraṇa sañjñakaṅgaḷappa ṣōḍaśaprakr̥tigaḷumapratyākhyāna krōdha-
māna māyā lōbhaṅgaḷembeṇṭuṁ kaṣāyaṅgaḷumaṁ napuṁsakavēdaṁ strīvē-
daṁ hāsya ratyarati śōka bhaya jugupsābhidhāna nōkaṣāyaṣaṭka puruṣa-
vēda sañjvaḷana krōdha māna māyā kaṣāyamendintivaṁ bēṟevēṟe pari-
viḍiyiṁ paḍalvaḍivinaṁ kiḍisi nivr̥tta sāmāyikacchēdōpasthāpanā śuddhi-
saṁyamānugatānivr̥ttisthānanāgi mattaṁ kiṟidubēgadiṁ sūkṣmasāmparāya-
saṁyamasampannaṁ sūkṣmasāmparāyasthānapraviṣṭakṣapakaṁ yathōkta pariṇā-
madiṁ sūkṣmalōbhakke viḷayamaṁ māḍi nirasta niravaśēṣa mōhanīyamaḷa-
kaḷaṅkaṁ yathākhyātacāritradoḷ  kūḍi pr̥thaktva vitarkavicāra prathama-
śukladhyānadiṁ kṣīṇakaṣāya vītarāgachadmastha guṇasthāna vyavasthitaṁ kiṟidu 
pottu viśramisi baḻiyamēkatva vitarkavicāramemba dvitayaśukladhyānadiṁ 
bahutara karmanirjaranāgi nidrāpracaḷagaḷanupāntyasamayadoḷ paṟipaḍisi 
caramasamayadoḷ jñānāvaraṇapañcakamuṁ darśanāvaraṇacatuṣkamuma-
nantarāyapañcakamuṁ nirmūḷamappantormodaloḷe kiḍisidāgaḷ

[va.] endu vandārubhavyasamūhaṁ parinirvāṇakriyākaḷāpamaṁ 
tīrci tamma nelegaḷge pōpudumanantaraṁ yuvarājamadhirājapadaviyaṁ paḍe-
